  /*
    This is kind of gross but let me explain.
    The triangle-down icon in the user lists menu component needs to be larger on small screens
    but Primer doesn't accept a responsive value for size.
    So instead we use CSS to override the size on small screens only, to match the ⭐ button beside it.
    The selector is written this way to avoid affecting other buttons inside the lists dropdown.
  */

      height: var(--control-medium-size);
      width: var(--control-medium-size);
      min-width: var(--control-medium-size);
    }

      right: auto !important;

</a></p>
<p dir="auto">A pytest plugin powered by VCR.py to record and replay HTTP traffic.</p>
<a name="user-content-features"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Features</h2><a id="user-content-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Features" href="#features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Straightforward <code>pytest.mark.vcr</code>, that reflects <code>VCR.use_cassettes</code> API;</li>
<li>Combining multiple VCR cassettes;</li>
<li>Network access blocking;</li>
<li>The <code>rewrite</code> recording mode that rewrites cassettes from scratch.</li>
</ul>
<a name="user-content-installation"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation</h2><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation" href="#installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="warning">⚠️</g-emoji> Incompatibility Warning</p>
<blockquote>
If you have <code>pytest-vcr</code> installed, please uninstall it before using <code>pytest-recording</code>, as the two plugins are incompatible.</blockquote>
<a name="user-content-usage"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Usage</h2><a id="user-content-usage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Usage" href="#usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>

<span class="pl-c"># cassettes/{module_name}/test_single.yaml will be used</span>
<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>.<span class="pl-c1">mark</span>.<span class="pl-c1">vcr</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">test_single</span>():
    <span class="pl-k">assert</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"http://httpbin.org/get"</span>).<span class="pl-c1">text</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">'{"get": true}'</span>

<span class="pl-c"># cassettes/{module_name}/example.yaml will be used</span>
<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>.<span class="pl-c1">mark</span>.<span class="pl-c1">default_cassette</span>(<span class="pl-s">"example.yaml"</span>)</span>
<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>.<span class="pl-c1">mark</span>.<span class="pl-c1">vcr</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">test_default</span>():
    <span class="pl-k">assert</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"http://httpbin.org/get"</span>).<span class="pl-c1">text</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">'{"get": true}'</span>

<span class="pl-c"># these cassettes will be used in addition to the default one</span>
<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>.<span class="pl-c1">mark</span>.<span class="pl-c1">vcr</span>(<span class="pl-s">"/path/to/ip.yaml"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"/path/to/get.yaml"</span>)</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">test_multiple</span>():
    <span class="pl-k">assert</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"http://httpbin.org/get"</span>).<span class="pl-c1">text</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">'{"get": true}'</span>
    <span class="pl-k">assert</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"http://httpbin.org/ip"</span>).<span class="pl-c1">text</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">'{"ip": true}'</span>

<span class="pl-c"># Make assertions based on the cassette calls/responses:</span>
<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>.<span class="pl-c1">mark</span>.<span class="pl-c1">vcr</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">test_call_count</span>(<span class="pl-s1">vcr</span>):
    <span class="pl-k">assert</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"http://httpbin.org/get"</span>).<span class="pl-c1">text</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">'{"get": true}'</span>
    <span class="pl-k">assert</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"http://httpbin.org/ip"</span>).<span class="pl-c1">text</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">'{"ip": true}'</span>
    <span class="pl-c"># See https://vcrpy.readthedocs.io/en/latest/advanced.html for more info</span>
    <span class="pl-c"># about the Cassette object:</span>
    <span class="pl-k">assert</span> <span class="pl-s1">vcr</span>.<span class="pl-c1">play_count</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span></pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="import pytest
import requests

# cassettes/{module_name}/test_single.yaml will be used
@pytest.mark.vcr
def test_single():
    assert requests.get(&quot;http://httpbin.org/get&quot;).text == '{&quot;get&quot;: true}'

# cassettes/{module_name}/example.yaml will be used
@pytest.mark.default_cassette(&quot;example.yaml&quot;)
@pytest.mark.vcr
def test_default():
    assert requests.get(&quot;http://httpbin.org/get&quot;).text == '{&quot;get&quot;: true}'

# these cassettes will be used in addition to the default one
@pytest.mark.vcr(&quot;/path/to/ip.yaml&quot;, &quot;/path/to/get.yaml&quot;)
def test_multiple():
    assert requests.get(&quot;http://httpbin.org/get&quot;).text == '{&quot;get&quot;: true}'
    assert requests.get(&quot;http://httpbin.org/ip&quot;).text == '{&quot;ip&quot;: true}'

# Make assertions based on the cassette calls/responses:
@pytest.mark.vcr
def test_call_count(vcr):
    assert requests.get(&quot;http://httpbin.org/get&quot;).text == '{&quot;get&quot;: true}'
    assert requests.get(&quot;http://httpbin.org/ip&quot;).text == '{&quot;ip&quot;: true}'
    # See https://vcrpy.readthedocs.io/en/latest/advanced.html for more info
    # about the Cassette object:
    assert vcr.play_count == 2" tabindex="0" role="button">
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-copy js-clipboard-copy-icon">

<p dir="auto">Run your tests:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre>pytest --record-mode=once test_network.py</pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="pytest --record-mode=once test_network.py" tabindex="0" role="button">
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-copy js-clipboard-copy-icon">
    <path d="M0 6.75C0 5.784.784 5 1.75 5h1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-1.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0v1.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 9.25 16h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 14.25Z"></path><path d="M5 1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h7.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 11h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 5 9.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-7.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25Z"></path>
</svg>
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-check js-clipboard-check-icon color-fg-success d-none">
    <path d="M13.78 4.22a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.06l-7.25 7.25a.75.75 0 0 1-1.06 0L2.22 9.28a.751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018L6 10.94l6.72-6.72a.75.75 0 0 1 1.06 0Z"></path>
</svg>
    </clipboard-copy>
  </div></div>
<a name="user-content-default-recording-mode"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Default recording mode</h3><a id="user-content-default-recording-mode" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Default recording mode" href="#default-recording-mode"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>pytest-recording</code> uses the <code>none</code> VCR recording mode by default to prevent unintentional network requests.
To allow them you need to pass a different recording mode (e.g. <code>once</code>) via the <code>--record-mode</code> CLI option to your test command.
See more information about available recording modes in the <a href="https://vcrpy.readthedocs.io/en/latest/usage.html#record-modes" rel="nofollow">official VCR documentation</a></p>
<a name="user-content-configuration"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Configuration</h3><a id="user-content-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Configuration" href="#configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can provide the recording configuration with the <code>vcr_config</code> fixture, which could be any scope - <code>session</code>,
<code>package</code>, <code>module</code>, or <code>function</code>. It should return a dictionary that will be passed directly to <code>VCR.use_cassettes</code>
under the hood.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>

<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>.<span class="pl-c1">fixture</span>(<span class="pl-s1">scope</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"module"</span>)</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">vcr_config</span>():
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> {<span class="pl-s">"filter_headers"</span>: [<span class="pl-s">"authorization"</span>]}</pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="import pytest

@pytest.fixture(scope=&quot;module&quot;)
def vcr_config():
    return {&quot;filter_headers&quot;: [&quot;authorization&quot;]}" tabindex="0" role="button">
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-copy js-clipboard-copy-icon">
    <path d="M0 6.75C0 5.784.784 5 1.75 5h1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-1.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0v1.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 9.25 16h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 14.25Z"></path><path d="M5 1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h7.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 11h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 5 9.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-7.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25Z"></path>
</svg>
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-check js-clipboard-check-icon color-fg-success d-none">
    <path d="M13.78 4.22a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.06l-7.25 7.25a.75.75 0 0 1-1.06 0L2.22 9.28a.751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018L6 10.94l6.72-6.72a.75.75 0 0 1 1.06 0Z"></path>

    </clipboard-copy>
  </div></div>
<p dir="auto">For more granular control you need to pass these keyword arguments to individual <code>pytest.mark.vcr</code> marks, and in this case
all arguments will be merged into a single dictionary with the following priority (low -&gt; high):</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>vcr_config</code> fixture</li>
<li>all marks from the most broad scope ("session") to the most narrow one ("function")</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Example:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>

<span class="pl-s1">pytestmark</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> [<span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>.<span class="pl-c1">mark</span>.<span class="pl-c1">vcr</span>(<span class="pl-s1">ignore_localhost</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">True</span>)]

<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>.<span class="pl-c1">fixture</span>(<span class="pl-s1">scope</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"module"</span>)</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">vcr_config</span>():
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> {<span class="pl-s">"filter_headers"</span>: [<span class="pl-s">"authorization"</span>]}

<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>.<span class="pl-c1">mark</span>.<span class="pl-c1">vcr</span>(<span class="pl-s1">filter_headers</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[])</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">test_one</span>():
    ...

<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>.<span class="pl-c1">mark</span>.<span class="pl-c1">vcr</span>(<span class="pl-s1">filter_query_parameters</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[<span class="pl-s">"api_key"</span>])</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">test_two</span>():
    ...</pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">

<p dir="auto">Resulting VCR configs for each test:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>test_one</code> - <code>{"ignore_localhost": True, "filter_headers": []}</code></li>
<li><code>test_two</code> - <code>{"ignore_localhost": True, "filter_headers": ["authorization"], "filter_query_parameters": ["api_key"]}</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">You can get access to the used <code>VCR</code> instance via <code>pytest_recording_configure</code> hook. It might be useful for registering
custom matchers, persisters, etc.:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-c"># conftest.py</span>

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">jurassic_matcher</span>(<span class="pl-s1">r1</span>, <span class="pl-s1">r2</span>):
    <span class="pl-k">assert</span> <span class="pl-s1">r1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">uri</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s1">r2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">uri</span> <span class="pl-c1">and</span> <span class="pl-s">"JURASSIC PARK"</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">r1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">body</span>, \
        <span class="pl-s">"required string (JURASSIC PARK) not found in request body"</span>

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">pytest_recording_configure</span>(<span class="pl-s1">config</span>, <span class="pl-s1">vcr</span>):
    <span class="pl-s1">vcr</span>.<span class="pl-c1">register_matcher</span>(<span class="pl-s">"jurassic"</span>, <span class="pl-s1">jurassic_matcher</span>)</pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="# conftest.py

<p dir="auto">You can disable the VCR.py integration entirely by passing the <code>--disable-recording</code> CLI option.</p>
<a name="user-content-rewrite-record-mode"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Rewrite record mode</h3><a id="user-content-rewrite-record-mode" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Rewrite record mode" href="#rewrite-record-mode"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">It is possible to rewrite a cassette from scratch and not extend it with new entries as it works now with the <code>all</code> record mode from VCR.py.</p>
<p dir="auto">However, it will rewrite only the default cassette and won't touch extra cassettes.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>

<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>.<span class="pl-c1">fixture</span>(<span class="pl-s1">scope</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"module"</span>)</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">vcr_config</span>():
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> {<span class="pl-s">"record_mode"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"rewrite"</span>}</pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="import pytest

@pytest.fixture(scope=&quot;module&quot;)
def vcr_config():
    return {&quot;record_mode&quot;: &quot;rewrite&quot;}" tabindex="0" role="button">

<a name="user-content-blocking-network-access"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Blocking network access</h3><a id="user-content-blocking-network-access" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Blocking network access" href="#blocking-network-access"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To have more confidence that your tests will not go over the wire, you can block it with <code>pytest.mark.block_network</code> mark:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>

<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>.<span class="pl-c1">mark</span>.<span class="pl-c1">block_network</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">test_multiple</span>():
    <span class="pl-k">assert</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"http://httpbin.org/get"</span>).<span class="pl-c1">text</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">'{"get": true}'</span>

...
<span class="pl-c"># in case of access</span>
<span class="pl-v">RuntimeError</span>: <span class="pl-v">Network</span> <span class="pl-c1">is</span> <span class="pl-s1">disabled</span></pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">

<p dir="auto">Besides marks, the network access could be blocked globally with <code>--block-network</code> command-line option.</p>
<p dir="auto">However, if VCR.py recording is enabled, the network is not blocked for tests with <code>pytest.mark.vcr</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Example:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>

<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>.<span class="pl-c1">mark</span>.<span class="pl-c1">vcr</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">test_multiple</span>():
    <span class="pl-k">assert</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"http://httpbin.org/get"</span>).<span class="pl-c1">text</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">'{"get": true}'</span></pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="import pytest

<p dir="auto">The network blocking feature supports <code>socket</code>-based transports and <code>pycurl</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">It is possible to allow access to specified hosts during network blocking:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>

<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>.<span class="pl-c1">mark</span>.<span class="pl-c1">block_network</span>(<span class="pl-s1">allowed_hosts</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[<span class="pl-s">"httpbin.*"</span>])</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">test_access</span>():
    <span class="pl-k">assert</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"http://httpbin.org/get"</span>).<span class="pl-c1">text</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">'{"get": true}'</span>
    <span class="pl-k">with</span> <span class="pl-s1">pytest</span>.<span class="pl-c1">raises</span>(<span class="pl-v">RuntimeError</span>, <span class="pl-s1">match</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">r"^Network is disabled$"</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"http://example.com"</span>)</pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="import pytest
import requests

@pytest.mark.block_network(allowed_hosts=[&quot;httpbin.*&quot;])
def test_access():
    assert requests.get(&quot;http://httpbin.org/get&quot;).text == '{&quot;get&quot;: true}'
    with pytest.raises(RuntimeError, match=r&quot;^Network is disabled$&quot;):
        requests.get(&quot;http://example.com&quot;)" tabindex="0" role="button">
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-copy js-clipboard-copy-icon">

<a name="user-content-test-isolation-for-package-maintainers"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Test Isolation for Package Maintainers</h2><a id="user-content-test-isolation-for-package-maintainers" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Test Isolation for Package Maintainers" href="#test-isolation-for-package-maintainers"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">When running pytest-based tests in a packaging environment, globally installed plugins can break test suites by
injecting unexpected hooks or fixtures (e.g. <code>pytest-pretty</code>) that your code isn’t designed for.</p>
<p dir="auto">To guarantee a clean, reproducible test run:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-shell-session notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-c1">export PYTEST_DISABLE_PLUGIN_AUTOLOAD=1</span>
<span class="pl-c1">export PYTEST_PLUGINS=pytest_httpbin.plugin,pytest_mock,pytest_recording.plugin</span></pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="export PYTEST_DISABLE_PLUGIN_AUTOLOAD=1
export PYTEST_PLUGINS=pytest_httpbin.plugin,pytest_mock,pytest_recording.plugin" tabindex="0" role="button">

      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-check js-clipboard-check-icon color-fg-success d-none">
    <path d="M13.78 4.22a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.06l-7.25 7.25a.75.75 0 0 1-1.06 0L2.22 9.28a.751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018L6 10.94l6.72-6.72a.75.75 0 0 1 1.06 0Z"></path>
</svg>
    </clipboard-copy>
  </div></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>PYTEST_DISABLE_PLUGIN_AUTOLOAD</strong>
Disables loading of any plugins via setuptools entry-points; only those you explicitly list
will be activated.</li>
<li><strong>PYTEST_PLUGINS</strong>
Comma-separated list of plugin modules pytest should load (the core plugin manager still
discovers builtin plugins and conftest.py).</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Include these exports in your package’s build or CI script so that system-wide pytest plugins
(e.g. linting, formatting, or unrelated test helpers) cannot interfere with your tests.</p>
<a name="user-content-python-support"></a>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Python support</h2><a id="user-content-python-support" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Python support" href="#python-support"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Pytest-recording supports:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>CPython 3.10, 3.11, 3.12, 3.13 and 3.14</li>
<li>PyPy 7.3 (3.11)</li>
